<script>
  function generatelucky() {
    let numbers = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
      numbers.push(Math.floor(Math.random() * 10)); // digits 0-9
    }

    let screen = document.getElementById("lucky-display");
    screen.innerText = "- - - - -"; // initial reset

    let j = 0;
    let timer = setInterval(() => {
      let currText = screen.innerText.split(" ");
      currText[j] = numbers[j]; // update one digit at a time
      screen.innerText = currText.join(" ");
      j++;
      if (j >= numbers.length) {
        clearInterval(timer);

        // show fortune message after completion
        document.getElementById("fortune-msg").innerText =
          "Nomor Keberuntunganmu 🎉: " + numbers.join(" ");
        document.getElementById("fortune-msg").style.display = "block";

        // lock button after single use
        document.getElementById("generate-btn").disabled = true;
        document.getElementById("generate-btn").innerText = "SELESAI";
      }
    }, 400); // 400ms delay per digit
  }
</script>
